{~f9r~}\n
{=Hand B takes over from Hand A to finish Sawles Warde. I have realised\n
yogh as z although it has somewhat the look of insular g. But it is\n
most like the form which the Bodley 34 scribe uses, which is made in\n
three strokes but is very stylised and can hardly any longer be called\n
insular g=}\n

{=The other texts have GODLEC and the context demands "goodness" rather\n
than "divinity". Perhaps the Royal scribe did not understand the system\n
of doubling the consonant to imply "god" with short vowel and leaving it\n
single to signal "good" with long vowel. Cf. similar misunderstanding in\n
hand A, St Katherine=}\n
